                 </p>\n\n                  </div>\n                  <div class=\"card-action\">\n                      <a class=\"waves-effect waves-green btn-flat\" target=\"_blank\"        </div>\n          </div>\n\n\n\n\n      \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n<div class=\"left col s12 m8 \">\n        <div class=\"card-panel\">\n          <div class=\"blue-text text-darken-2\">\n\n<p><span
